<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерзкий.html>ме́рзкий</a> (6622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьрзъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭrzŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзнуть.html>мёрзнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjórznutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moróz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзкий.html>ме́рзкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mérzkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мерзе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мерзе́й</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ме́рзче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vile, disgusting, abominable, nasty, odious</li></ol>

***мерить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́рить</a> (12129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měriti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">méritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерить.html>изме́рить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поме́рить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to measure</li>
<li>to try on</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<dl><dt>Verbs</dt></dl>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ме́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>рить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — померить, <a href = vnd.unilang:измерить.html>изме́рить</a>, замерить.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> просторечный <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> словообразования <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1a: <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> мерять — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́ряю</a>, ме́рял, <a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́ряющий</a>, ме́рявший, <a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́ряя</a>, ме́ряв</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мер-</b> |  суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b> |  глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a> (17491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьркнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭrknuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mь̀rknǫti</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морока.html>морок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">morok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мрак.html>мрак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mrak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mercátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mérknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркнуть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to grow dark/dim</li>
<li>to fade, to wane
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó sláva pomérkla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his fame dwindled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pale <i>(before)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнущий</a> (17491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***мертвенный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мертвенный.html>ме́ртвенный</a> (21401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвенный.html>ме́ртвенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mértvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ме́ртвеннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ме́ртвенней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ме́ртвеннейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deadly pale, ghastly, lifeless</li>
<li>deathly</li></ol>

***мертвый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвый</a> (6625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьrtvъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mr̥twós</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mr̥tós</i>, ultimately from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to die</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjórtvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мертве́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мертве́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjórtvaja</b> tóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dead center</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjórtvyj</b> čas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">after-dinner rest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lifeless</li></ol>

***мерцание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерцание.html>мерца́ние</a> (17739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцание.html>мерца́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mercánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцание.html>мерца́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцание.html>мерца́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцание.html>мерца́ний</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>мер</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ца́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a></b> ➔ мерц + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> + <b>ниj</b> + е (суффиксальный).

***мерцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a> (5013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьрцати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭrcati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mérknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mercátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shimmer, to twinkle, to glimmer, to flicker</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцающий.html>мерца́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mercájuščij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mercátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***месить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a> (18447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měsiti</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mesítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to knead</li>
<li>to mix with water <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of clay</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***месса.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месса.html>ме́сса</a> (23567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">messe</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">messa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Messe</i>. All from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dismissed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ite, missa est</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">go, (the assembly) is dismissed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, last words of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman_Rite" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Roman Rite">Roman Rite</a> of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catholic_Church" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Catholic Church">Catholic Church</a>.
</p>

***местечко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>местечко</a> (4822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Diminutive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésto</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">place, (dialectal) city</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or calqued from another Slavic language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">miasteczko</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mestéčko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>A small village or town on the territory of the former <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish%E2%80%93Lithuanian_Commonwealth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth">Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth</a>.</li>
<li>A shtetl, small Jewish village.</li></ol>

<p><b>мес<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>те́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">мѣстечко</span>)

***мести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>мести</a> (18722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mestì</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>мести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмести.html>подмести́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замести.html>замести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sweep</li>
<li>to scatter</li>
<li>to swirl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to snow strongly, to blizzard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>Метёт</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Metjót</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There's a snowstorm.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***место.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>место</a> (106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*město</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mésto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>мест</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gluxóje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">backwoods</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zadétʹ bolʹnóje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut to the quick</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">znatʹ svojó <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to know one’s place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">imétʹ <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take place, to happen; to exist</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меняться.html>меня́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́ми</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjátʹsja <b>mestámi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">switch places</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́шем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na vášem <b>méste</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">if I were you</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>mestáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the local level; in the provinces</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщее</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">óbščeje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">banality, platitude</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">отхо́жее <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otxóžeje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">outhouse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадочный.html>поса́дочное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posádočnoje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">seat, seating place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">прису́тственное <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prisútstvennoje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">public office (in the Russian Empire)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sláboje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">weak spot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теплый.html>тёплое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tjóploje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gravy train, soft job</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>) region, area
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ли</a> когда́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тих</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́х</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy byváli kogdá-libo v étix <b>mestáx</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Have you ever been in these parts?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>site, scene
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:битва.html>би́твы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mésto</b> bítvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">battle site</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>job, position
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проработать.html>прорабо́тал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja na étom <b>méste</b> prorabótal dvádcatʹ let.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve been at this job for twenty years.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>piece (<i>of luggage</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>мест</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko u Vas <b>mest</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How many pieces of luggage do you have?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>room, space
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сувенир.html>сувени́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чемодан.html>чемода́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a></strong>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na ješčó odín suvenír v čemodáne prósto ne xvatílo mesta.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There was simply no room for another souvenir in the suitcase.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нства</a></i>.
